<gmap_id>0x80c2d205a2826e45:0x41e26e211cf80bda</gmap_id>< review>
Their food is so fresh and tasty. Their staff is so friendly and efficient. Their prices are a bargain for what you get.
Today I got the Camarones Costa Azul combo plate. It was just perfect,  shrimps were tasty and moist and the bacon wrap crispy and fried to perfection.
I highly recommend this place, they also have a small selection of beer to wash down your food. Once you try their food and service you'll forget you're in a fast food place ( I can't actually believe this is primarily a burger/taco joint ü§î).
But heads up! I recommend you order online or by phone ahead of time, that way you'll save a lot of time and avoid the lines.</review>

<Text>It is said that the Rosewood Post-Acute Rehabilitation Center in Carmichael was awarded, by some accrediting agency, Five Stars in recognition of its provision of superior health care. Admitted in 2017, my wife is a long-term resident of the facility. Based upon my wife‚Äôs and my direct experience with the quality of care offered by the Center, I also award Five Stars to the facility but with a twist. Here is my take of that.

First Star is earned by the CNA‚Äôs who provide the daily hands-on care of the residents. There are several who are outstanding in attentiveness, who assure extra help whenever needed, and who are kind and unflappable. Their work is not easy, probably the most difficult of daily tasks; and they are under-appreciated. I would nominate ‚Äòthe several‚Äô for special recognition.

Second Star goes to the nursing staff; many are especially caring. The nurses make sure everything runs smoothly, and some of them are really effective in this regard. Upon admission, my wife was diagnosed as being in her death process. I credit the nurses who took care of her and brought her back to living and continue to do so. Of course, my wife‚Äôs power also assured recovery. She now is stable and enjoys life much more ‚Äì a true miracle of medical science and care!

Third Star is for all the personnel who work hard to keep the facility clean, well lighted, and fully functional. While probably always ignored and forgotten, these personnel provide the essentials for openness and welcoming of residents and visitors. The maintenance, kitchen, activities, and social services staffs round out these essentials for a smooth operation of all functions. Rosewood is very effective here when all parties communicate.

Fourth Star has to do with creating and maintaining an overall environment that is open, clean, well lighted, and friendly. That environment is exemplified in the attitudes and good cheer of all staff and residents. Happy environment means good care and good health.

Fifth Star belongs to the administration of the facility, to the top management. Rosewood is now under new ownership, and its Administrator provides the right kind of leadership ‚Äì including an hands-on approach, his accessibility ‚Äì which was most impressive to me. I once had a conversation with him about what it means to be a resident and what it means to their families. He spoke about his philosophy of caring that is supportive of life, well being, and rehabilitation. He spoke of essential caring and sensitive support for the elderly and severely infirm who face their end of life. He said the purpose, then, of Rosewood was to develop a place for confronting such difficult human conditions. I was deeply moved by his views and saw that the grand improvements made at Rosewood were due to him.

Finally, the stars add up to five as the ultimate accolade. That does not mean there are no concerns or problems. What it does mean is that solutions will be found. Of that, I am sure.<//Text>< pics>

DO NOT TAKE ANYONE YOU LOVE, & DO NOT GO YOURSELF TO ROSEWOOD REHAB IN CARMICHAEL.

They expected my arrival & yet my bed was bare, no sheets or blankets.  I had to lay down on the plastic mattress until they got it together.

But the real problem was upon intake, they check you for bruises or bedsores.  I had none of the above & realized they had to see for themselves, so I complied.

However, the nurse (her name was Story), did something I never could have anticipated.  Without warning, instead of looking for bruises & bedsores, she reached out & grabbed me with BOTH HANDS, in a Very, Very personal spot & manhandled me.  I felt violated & told her to stop.

Her response was to threaten me & told me that she was going to continue what she was doing or I would be kicked out of the rehab center.

Another nurse came in & asked if I refused to comply.  I told her that they can look, but they cannot touch me in the personal manner that they just did.  This nurse also threatened to kick me out of the rehab center.

Then a man came in claiming he was the head nurse.  He asked me if I was going to comply and I told him they could look, but not touch in the matter that they previously did.

I told him that I was more than willing to comply with what was necessary but not to be violated. I told him I had no bed sores or bruises in the areas they wanted to look, & I would be more than willing to sign a waiver to verify that information.

As with the previous two nurses he told me that if I did not comply I had to leave. Not long after that an ambulance company came to pick me up and take me away.

Now my doctors and social workers are trying to get me into another rehab facility that does not inappropriately touch their patients. But they cannot get me into rehab because Rosewood Rehab Center listed me as non-compliant.

A quick translation for non-compliant means I am not a Cooperative patient. That was a brutal lie. I was more than willing to cooperate but I was not willing to be violated. What they did amounts to sexual abuse.

Now I am home trying to recover from my surgery and I've tried several times to call the director of nursing and also the administrative office director, Michael Moore. I left a few nessages for Michael.  No response.

It's so funny how you cannot get a response back, no matter how many times you call, when the facility does not want to admit they are in the wrong. I have been told on multiple occasions this is medical malpractice and to get the lawyers ready.

It has been confirmed on multiple fronts that the nurses do not have the right to touch you in an inappropriate way and at the very least should have asked permission.

They had no permission because what they were doing was wrong.

So I hope everybody reads this post and please whatever you do don't you ever go to this facility and don't let a loved one go to this facility.

If they did that to me, a woman capable of speaking up for herself, can you only imagine what they would do to somebody who is more elderly and not able to speak on their own behalf? What do they do to the patients when the families aren't around to watch?

Honestly I'm scared. I am more scared for the people still in Rosewood rehab facility in Carmichael, because I am now safe from their Wrath.

The worst they could do to me is stop me from getting the care I need to recover by listing me as non-compliant. And in itself that has been devastating.<//Text>

< review>
If you're looking for a very good orthodox teaching in Catholicism this is the place to be.  Fr. Robert is a great shepherd of the flock along with the associate priests.  We cannot thank them enough for their priesthood and their ministry.  These men are great gifts to the community.
Also, for Catholics who have plenty of questions to their faith, there's the bible study every Monday at 7pm in the parish center.  You will love our Lord even more as you know Him.  If we only realize it, there is not enough time in this life to fully know our GOD.  No room for boredom if you walk with the Lord and plenty of work and learning to be done to fulfill our mission and to proclaim our Lord's glory.  :)</review>

< text>
Machine learning Class sucked.  This was the second awful experience I had with coursera:  MongoDB class was also impossible to complete.

I watched the first two weeks video's, but after logging out/back in they were no longer listed as having been watched.  Navigating the site is a pain as there is such a high latency that any click I made took so long to respond that frustration was immediately the result of navigating the coursera site and course pages.  Videos played but would automatically bypass their built-in quizzes and just play the videos without allowing me to perform the quiz portion, so it was impossible to determine if I was on the correct path.

Video's that were useful were impossible to navigate as attempting to fast forwarding or rewind to a previously watched section was nearly impossible... the settings bar never(or, hardly ever... i had to reload the page if i wanted to move around in the video because watching the videos made my browser wholly unresponsive...) shows and makes it impossible to navigate the videos.  The pause/unpause function work fine, just navigating is frustratingly slow. I gave up on watching the vector videos over and over... they were not that informative and did not have any real content, so watching them over and over was a waste of my time.  long, and drawn out 15 minute video's could have been bypassed with a printout that could be read and fully comprehended in ~10-15 seconds, and speeding up the videos using the speed setting makes the web pages completely un-navigable.

the quizzes are a joke: repeat the same questions over and over until you get the correct answers.  If you do not get the correct answers, there are no methods for you to learn what you did wrong: you are only told that you provided a wrong answer and re-directed to watch the same videos which you obviously did not understand in the first place- over and over again- until you "do" "get it", which for me was never.

After two futile attempts- and a major wast of my precious free time- I can not recommend Coursera classes to anyone serious about learning.  Use Youtube; it will be easier to watch their videos.< /text>
